# Pound Testing
-----------------------------------

We're now using lighttpd instead of boa for the web server:

In a Chrome browser, try to access http://<target ip>
```
You should see the lighttpd, "It Works!" page
```

In a Chrome browser, try to access https://<target ip>
```
You should see "This site canâ€™t be reached"
```

On the target, now start Pound,
```
pound &
```

Wait a minute or so and then in a Chrome browser, try to access https://<target ip>
```
You should see "Your connection is not private" and be able to "Proceed to 192.168.1.18 (unsafe)" to see the "It Works!" page via https
```

Also, perform the FunkLoad test:

From host machine, set up FunkLoad:
```
sudo pip install ez_setup distribute setuptools
sudo pip install git+https://github.com/nuxeo/FunkLoad.git
```

Modify Simple.conf to have correct IP addresses of target board:
```
cd <somewhere>/buildroot-testsuites/pound/webserver/testcase/simple

nano Simple.conf

set:

serverip=<target ip>
url=http://<target ip>/test
```

Change scp_cmd to be correct path for lighttpd in test_Simple_arm.py:
```
This:

scp_cmd='scp -rp ../test root@'+serverip+':/var/www/'

Should now be:

scp_cmd='scp -rp ../test root@'+serverip+':/www/pages'
```

From the host machine
```
python test_Simple_arm.py
```
